\label{tab:failed_toil_local}
\begin{longtable}{p{0.35\textwidth} >{\raggedright\arraybackslash}p{0.6\textwidth}}

\endfirsthead
\toprule
\textbf{ID} & \textbf{Description} \\

\endhead
\seqsplit{exprtool\_file\_literal} & Test file literal output created by ExpressionTool \\
\seqsplit{filename\_with\_hash\_mark} & Test for correct handling of URL-quoting in filename to refer to filename containing a hash mark \\
\seqsplit{scatter\_embedded\_subworkflow} & Test simple scatter over an embedded subworkflow \\
\seqsplit{stdin\_from\_directory\_literal\_with\_local\_file} & Pipe to stdin from user provided local File via a Directory literal \\
\seqsplit{stdin\_shorcut} & Test command execution in with stdin and stdout redirection using stdin shortcut \\
